# MIGRATION_LOG — per-step commit log of the consolidation

<!--
ROLE: A flat, ordered table of every atomic step executed against
      MIGRATION_PLAN.md. One row per atomic step / commit. Tracks: step
      ID, date, commit hash, what was done, validation passed, reviewer
      (if any), any deviations from the plan.
UPDATE POLICY: Append-only. Each commit that completes a P-step appends
      one row in the same atomic commit. Never reorder; never delete
      rows; corrections go into a separate "Corrections" section below.
TRIGGER: Every atomic migration step. Initialised retroactively for
      P0.1–P0.2 in P0.7.
-->

(2) `def:refmap` — a refinement map `E_{P\to P'}` is required to be an isometry (`E^\dagger E = id`) per the canonical `def:refmap` statement (`summary.tex:411`; `GLOSSARY.md:674-693`); this file proves the matrix-coordinate companion of the *componentwise* characterisation of that isometry condition: in any chosen orthonormal basis of the coarse and fine Hilbert spaces, the global identity `E_{P\to P'}^{\dagger} E_{P\to P'} = id_{A_P}` is equivalent to the columnwise orthonormality of the basis matrix of `E_{P\to P'}` — i.e. each column has unit norm and distinct columns are orthogonal, `\sum_b \overline{E_{ba}} E_{ba'} = \delta_{aa'}`; the bidirectional `matrix_component_orthogonality_iff` decomposes the single global Hom-sector isometry equation into one scalar equation per coarse-index pair, giving the per-component breakdown of `def:refmap`'s isometry constraint; this is precisely the "compositional structure" piece of the supporting infrastructure that GLOSSARY `def:refmap` Translation map CAD section explicitly names — verbatim: "`LinearAlgebra/Postcompose.lean` (P4.8) and `LinearAlgebra/Component.lean` (P4.9) for compositional structure" (`GLOSSARY.md:717`) — supporting infrastructure for `LinearAlgebra/FineGraining.lean` at P4.11, where this componentwise characterisation underwrites entrywise verification of the `FiniteFineGraining` instance's `E†E = id` condition; (2) `def:RG-amp` (GLOSSARY.md:1592) — the OPE/RG amplitude ansatz `β^a_{b₁⋯b_r}(ρ) ∼ Γ^a_{b₁⋯b_r} ρ^{h_a - ∑ h_{b_i}}` per `summary.tex:1875`; this file provides the abstract finite-dimensional "no-mixing scalar formula" companion to the polar-decomposition canonical-section framework of `LinearAlgebra/Polar.lean` (P4.3): for a single retained coarse label (the `PUnit` codomain) and a fine vector of OPE amplitudes `β : ι → ℂ`, the canonical section of the polar decomposition reduces to the closed-form scalar amplitudes `NoMixingAmplitude β i = star (β i) / √(∑ ν, |β_ν|²)` (with denominator `NoMixingDenominator β = ∑ i, Complex.normSq (β i)` and its non-negativity `NoMixingDenominator_nonneg`); the unit-norm condition for this amplitude family, `∑ i, star (NoMixingAmplitude β i) * NoMixingAmplitude β i = 1` (`noMixingAmplitude_normalised`), is precisely the scalar no-mixing normalisation underlying the handoff no-mixing corollary (`summary.tex` Cor.~`cor:nomix` at `summary.tex:1930`); the matrix-level reconstruction is provided by `NoMixingBlockingMatrix β : Matrix PUnit ι ℂ` (the row vector `β`, playing the role of the blocking map) and `NoMixingPolarR β : Matrix PUnit PUnit ℂ` (the `1×1` `(R)`-block equal to `1 / √(∑ ν, |β_ν|²)` from the polar decomposition); together they yield the matrix entry identity `((NoMixingBlockingMatrix β).conjTranspose * NoMixingPolarR β) i unit = NoMixingAmplitude β i` (`noMixingPolarSection_entry`) and the isometry equation `((NoMixingBlockingMatrix β)^† * NoMixingPolarR β)^† * ((NoMixingBlockingMatrix β)^† * NoMixingPolarR β) = 1` (`noMixingPolarSection_isometry`, conditional on `NoMixingDenominator β ≠ 0`); this is precisely the GLOSSARY-pre-registered binding "general no-mixing scalar formula in `LinearAlgebra/NoMixing.lean` (P4.10)" — verbatim — for `def:RG-amp` (`GLOSSARY.md:1619`), paired with the abstract polar-decomposition canonical-section framework in `LinearAlgebra/Polar.lean` (P4.3) and the Fibonacci-specific RG-decorated amplitude formulas slated for `Fibonacci/RGNoMixing.lean` at Phase 5 P5.14. **No new GLOSSARY entries added** (per orchestrator instruction; both referenced terms already exist in `GLOSSARY.md`: `conv:basics:130`, `def:RG-amp:1592`; `def:RG-amp` Translation map CAD section at `GLOSSARY.md:1619` explicitly names `LinearAlgebra/NoMixing.lean (P4.10)` as the canonical CAD anchor for the "general no-mixing scalar formula" — so this commit completes the GLOSSARY-pre-registered slug-to-file binding for the abstract no-mixing companion of `def:RG-amp`; same precedent as P4.4/P4.5/P4.6 for the `def:refmap` Tensor/TensorPower/HeterogeneousTensor trio, P4.7 for the `def:ascending` Trace.lean anchor, and P4.8/P4.9 for the `def:refmap` Postcompose/Component pair). **Formalisation.lean update:** appended one line `import Formalisation.LinearAlgebra.NoMixing` immediately after the existing `import Formalisation.LinearAlgebra.Component` line (Formalisation.lean grows 20 lines → 21 lines per the P4.1 plan note "per-file `import Formalisation.LinearAlgebra.<file>` lines will be appended here in those commits"). **`lake build` (first run, post-port):** "Built Formalisation.LinearAlgebra.NoMixing (8.3s)" → "Built Formalisation (5.6s)" → "Build completed successfully (8444 jobs)"; (2) `def:refine` (GLOSSARY.md:644) — the partition refinement order `P \preceq P'` of `summary.tex:403` of the directed set `(P, \preceq)`; per the Translation map CAD section at `GLOSSARY.md:668`, this file is the canonical CAD anchor: "CAD's coherent-refinement structure (`LinearAlgebra/CoherentSystem.lean`, Phase 4 P4.12) implements the categorical compatible-family axioms abstractly but does not implement the partition combinatorics"; the abstract directed-set structure is reduced to a totally-ordered chain `(ℕ, ≤)`: the structure's two indices `n m : ℕ` with the hypothesis `n ≤ m` stand in for `P \preceq P'` and the cellwise-local partition combinatorics is suppressed (the `\bigotimes_{I \in P}` cellwise decomposition of `def:refmap` lives in `LinearAlgebra/Tensor.lean` (P4.4), `TensorPower.lean` (P4.5), `HeterogeneousTensor.lean` (P4.6); the coherent-family abstraction here is a `n ≤ m`-indexed compatible tower sitting above those tensor-product cellwise-local building blocks). (3) `def:refmap` (GLOSSARY.md:674) — the refinement map `E_{P\to P'}: A_P \to A_{P'}` of `summary.tex:411`, required to be an isometry (`E_{P\to P'}^{\dagger} E_{P\to P'} = id_{A_P}`) and cellwise local; the `CoherentMatrixSystem.map` field `map : ℕ → ℕ → Matrix ι ι ℂ` IS the matrix realisation of `E_{P\to P'}` for the `(ℕ, ≤)`-indexed totally-ordered chain simplification of the partition directed-set; the `isometry` field `(S.map n m).conjTranspose * S.map n m = 1` IS the isometry condition `E_{P\to P'}^{\dagger} E_{P\to P'} = id_{A_P}` of `def:refmap`; the matrix-algebra-level packaging `FiniteFineGraining` (per the `def:refmap` canonical CAD anchor at `GLOSSARY.md:717`, `LinearAlgebra/FineGraining.lean`, P4.11) packages a SINGLE refinement map; `CoherentMatrixSystem` here packages a coherent FAMILY of refinement maps `{map n m : n ≤ m}` along the `(ℕ, ≤)` chain. The cellwise-local tensor-product structure of `def:refmap` is handled separately in `Tensor.lean` (P4.4), `TensorPower.lean` (P4.5), `HeterogeneousTensor.lean` (P4.6). (4) `def:indlim` (GLOSSARY.md:725) — the inductive limit `\Hh_\infty^{W} := \overline{\varinjlim_{P} \Hh_P^{W}}` of `summary.tex:427`, built from a `def:indlim` compatible family of refinement maps satisfying `E_{P\to P} = id` and `E_{P'\to P''} E_{P\to P'} = E_{P\to P''}`; this file is the GLOSSARY-pre-registered canonical CAD anchor for `def:indlim` — verbatim per the Translation map CAD section at `GLOSSARY.md:771`: "`LinearAlgebra/CoherentSystem.lean` (Phase 4 P4.12) — compatible-family axioms (`E_{P→P}=id`, `E_{P'→P''} ∘ E_{P→P'} = E_{P→P''}`) proved. Hilbert completion of the algebraic direct limit not in CAD scope (CAD is finite-dim coordinate-only)"; the structure `CoherentMatrixSystem ι` packages the compatible family as: `map n n = 1` (`id_map` field; the `E_{P\to P} = id` condition), `map m l * map n m = map n l` for `n ≤ m ≤ l` (`comp_map` field; the compatibility / associativity-of-refinement equation `E_{P'\to P''} E_{P\to P'} = E_{P\to P''}`), and the per-map isometry field; the `coherentAscending` and `coherentLogicalLift` ascending / lifting channels are functorial along the `(ℕ, ≤)` chain — the `coherentAscending_comp` theorem (`coherentAscending S n m (coherentAscending S m l O) = coherentAscending S n l O`) and `coherentLogicalLift_comp` theorem (the dual `coherentLogicalLift S m l (coherentLogicalLift S n m O) = coherentLogicalLift S n l O`) discharge the compatibility-along-composition of the channel structure built on top of the family; the `coherentAscending_unital` theorem `coherentAscending S n m 1 = 1` discharges the unital identity of the `def:ascending` ascending channel `\Aa(id_{A_{P'}}) = id_{A_P}` at every level of the chain; the `coherentLogicalLift_id` theorem `coherentLogicalLift S n n O = O` discharges the `n = m` base case via the `id_map` field; the Hilbert completion `\overline{\varinjlim_P \Hh_P^W}` of the algebraic direct limit is explicitly OUT OF CAD SCOPE per the canonical-anchor line — CAD works at the matrix-algebra level (finite-dimensional coordinate-only); the downstream analytic infrastructure (Hilbert completion as a topological closure) is not formalised in this repo. **No new GLOSSARY entries added** (per orchestrator instruction; all four referenced terms already exist in `GLOSSARY.md`: `conv:basics:130`, `def:refine:644`, `def:refmap:674`, `def:indlim:725`; The `structure FiniteSkeletalFusionData` realises clauses (i)+(ii)+(vi) of the seven-clause `def:fuscat` definition at `summary.tex:113`: field `Label : Type u` with the `[labelFintype : Fintype Label]` + `[labelDecidableEq : DecidableEq Label]` typeclass instances realises clause (i) finite `Irr(C)`; field `unit : Label` realises clause (ii) distinguished simple unit `1 ∈ Irr(C)`; field `fusionMultiplicity : Label → Label → Label → Nat` with the `leftUnit` + `rightUnit` field equations realises clause (vi) nonneg-integer fusion multiplicities `N_{ab}^{c}` at the skeletal-coordinate level (the unit-law equations being the skeletal shadows of `a ⊗ 1 ≅ a ≅ 1 ⊗ a`). Derivations from clauses (i)+(ii)+(vi); no new categorical content: `totalFusionMultiplicity a b := ∑ c, fusionMultiplicity a b c` is a derived sum over the third multiplicity index (a quantum-dimension-shaped total channel count); `MultiplicityFree : Prop := ∀ a b c, fusionMultiplicity a b c ≤ 1` is the intrinsic condition (foreshadows [[def:fib]] and [[def:ising]] but is itself a property of the data, NOT a new defined term — no new GLOSSARY entry needed); the six derived unit-law theorems (`leftUnit_same`, `leftUnit_different`, `rightUnit_same`, `rightUnit_different`, `total_leftUnit`, `total_rightUnit`) unfold `leftUnit` / `rightUnit` onto the diagonal (`c = a`, value `1`) and off-diagonal (`c ≠ a`, value `0`) cases and sum to recover the unital identities `∑_c N_{1a}^{c} = 1 = ∑_c N_{a1}^{c}`. (2) `conv:basics` (GLOSSARY.md:130) — Notation and conventions. The complex-vector-space default is NOT invoked at this integer-multiplicity skeletal level (the multiplicity table takes values in `Nat`); the load-bearing role of `conv:basics` here is typeclass-side: the `[Fintype Label]` + `[DecidableEq Label]` instances are the canonical Mathlib realisations of the "finite, equality-decidable label set" substrate; `∑ c : C.Label, ...` in `totalFusionMultiplicity` and the `classical` tactic in the two `total_*` theorems are the Mathlib renderings of the categorical "sum over `Irr(C)`" used implicitly throughout `summary.tex` §3-§4. This file is the GLOSSARY-pre-registered canonical CAD support construction for `def:Hlatt` — verbatim per the Translation map CAD section at `GLOSSARY.md:497`: "Supporting CAD constructions on the same `H_N^W` skeleton: `Foundations/DirectSumCoordinates.lean` (Phase 5 P5.2) for the Σ↔Π sum equivalence". The Σ↔Π sum equivalence is realised here as `sigmaPiLinearEquiv : (Sigma κ → ℂ) ≃ₗ[ℂ] (∀ i, κ i → ℂ)`: the sigma-indexed coordinate vector `Sigma κ → ℂ` is the flattened coordinate description of a finite biproduct `⊕_i V_i` (each summand `V_i` itself coordinatised by `κ i → ℂ`); the dependent product `∀ i, κ i → ℂ` is the same finite biproduct viewed as a Pi-type of per-component coordinate functions; the linear equivalence `sigmaPiLinearEquiv` and its symmetric inverse `piToSigma` interchange the two presentations. This is the finite-vector-space skeleton behind the categorical direct-sum Hom expansion in `def:Hlatt`'s `Hh_N = ⊕_W Hh_N^W` (`summary.tex:285`): once bases have been chosen in each charge-sector summand `Hh_N^W` (with `Hh_N^W ≅ (κ W → ℂ)` for some per-sector coordinate index `κ W`), the full `N`-site space's coordinates `Hh_N ≅ (Sigma κ → ℂ)` are interchangeable with the per-sector coordinate family `∀ W, κ W → ℂ`. The coordinate biproduct structure is realised by `componentInclusion` / `componentProjection` linear maps and the identity `sum_componentInclusion_projection : (∑ i, componentInclusion i (componentProjection i x)) = x` (the coordinate-level reconstruction of `x ∈ ⊕_i V_i` from its components). The cardinality identity `card_sigma_components : Fintype.card (Sigma κ) = ∑ i, Fintype.card (κ i)` is the dimension formula `dim (⊕_i V_i) = ∑_i dim V_i` at the coordinate level — the finite dimension of `def:Hlatt`'s `Hh_N = ⊕_W Hh_N^W`. The associated categorical biproducts, Hom spaces, and tensor structure are OUT OF SCOPE per the original module docstring's disclaimer at source lines 6–10 ("It does not construct categorical biproducts or Hom spaces") and the canonical-anchor line at `GLOSSARY.md:497` (which delimits this file to the coordinate-skeleton level); the categorical `H_N^W` realisation is supplied separately at P5.6 `ProjectDefinitions.lean::IndefiniteParticleSectorCoordinates`. (2) `conv:basics` (GLOSSARY.md:130) — Notation and conventions. The complex-vector-space default ("Vector spaces are complex unless otherwise stated") is invoked throughout: every coordinate space is `→ ℂ`; the linear equivalence `sigmaPiLinearEquiv` and the linear maps `componentInclusion` / `componentProjection` are explicitly `ℂ`-linear (`≃ₗ[ℂ]` / `→ₗ[ℂ]`). The dagger / categorical adjoint appears in coordinate form via Mathlib's `star` typeclass: the three standard finite coordinate pairings `sigmaCoordinatePairing`, `piCoordinatePairing`, `componentCoordinatePairing` are all `∑_{indices} star (x _) * y _`, i.e. `<x|y> := ∑ (x*) y` (the second-argument-linear physics convention). The "categorical adjoint = complex conjugate transpose for matrices" clause of `conv:basics` is realised explicitly in `componentProjection_adjoint_inclusion` and `componentProjection_adjoint_inclusion_right`: the projection `componentProjection i` is the (Mathlib `star`-pairing) adjoint of the inclusion `componentInclusion i` with respect to the standard coordinate pairings — the coordinate-level statement that "the component projection of an orthogonal finite direct sum is the adjoint of the corresponding inclusion". The `noncomputable section` opening (source line 16) is the standard Mathlib idiom when working with `ℂ`-linear maps depending on classical decidability (here via `DecidableEq` instance arguments). The `∑ i : ι, ...`, `∑ k : κ i, ...`, `∑ s : Sigma κ, ...` summation notations are Mathlib's `Finset.sum` / `Fintype.sum` renderings of the categorical "sum over indexing set" used implicitly throughout `summary.tex` §4 in `def:Hlatt`'s biproduct expansion. The `classical` tactic in the isometry / pairing lemmas is the Mathlib rendering of "all our finite-dim coordinate manipulations are classical". **No new GLOSSARY entries added** (per orchestrator instruction; both referenced terms already exist: `def:Hlatt:447`, `conv:basics:130`; ONE of the two slugs has an explicit pre-bound P5.2 DirectSumCoordinates.lean canonical-CAD-anchor line at `GLOSSARY.md:497` (`def:Hlatt`'s Translation map CAD section names this file verbatim) — this commit completes the SINGLE GLOSSARY-pre-registered slug-to-file binding for `def:Hlatt`'s "supporting CAD construction" entry). **Formalisation.lean update:** inserted one line `import Formalisation.Foundations.DirectSumCoordinates` immediately BEFORE the existing `import Formalisation.Foundations.SkeletalFusion` line (alphabetical within the Foundations block: `D` < `S`), preserving the Phase-5 import-ordering convention established at P5.1 (Foundations BEFORE LinearAlgebra) AND the within-block flat alphabetical convention; `Formalisation.lean` grows 26 lines → 27 lines. **`lake build`** (post-port): "Built Formalisation.Foundations.DirectSumCoordinates (7.9s)" → "Built Formalisation (5.8s)" → "Build completed successfully (8450 jobs)"; exit 0; wall clock 24.189s real / 21.508s user / 8.902s sys. The vacuum role is played by the abstract `vacuum : α` parameter (unconstrained at this generic level; the canonical Fibonacci instantiation `vacuum := one` is deferred to the bd-tracked `Fibonacci/Configurations.lean` follow-up cft-anyons-5tm.3; the canonical Ising instantiation is similarly deferred). **The GLOSSARY-pre-registered reverse-decoupling caveat at GLOSSARY.md:536 (the parenthetical "Configurations.lean currently imports `Fibonacci.FusionRules`; must be reverse-decoupled before migration (P5.3 covers this)") is DISCHARGED by this commit:** the import line `import Formalisation.Fibonacci.FusionRules` at CAD source line 2 is REMOVED, and the `import Mathlib` at CAD source line 1 is the ONLY import in this file (verified by the D-gate `grep -E "^import.*Fibonacci"` returning empty). (2) `conv:basics` (GLOSSARY.md:130) — Notation and conventions. The canonical statement at `summary.tex:76` fixes that "`\one` denotes the categorical unit object (also called the \emph{vacuum} simple)". This file's abstract `vacuum : α` parameter throughout `Config.particleNumber`, `Config.constant`, and the four particle-number lemmas is the GLOSSARY `conv:basics` `\one` / "vacuum simple" — the distinguished label whose count is excluded from the particle number. The fact that the parameter is left abstract here (rather than fixed to a specific label like the Fibonacci `one` or the Ising `psi_zero`) is the generic-over-fusion-data design choice that enables this file to serve as the shared substrate for both the Fibonacci and Ising fusion-category instantiations downstream; the instance-specific specialisations are deferred to the per-instance files. The `DecidableEq α` typeclass requirement in `Config.particleNumber` and each of the four particle-number lemmas is the standard Mathlib discharge of the `cfg i ≠ vacuum` predicate's decidability — a non-substantive infrastructure constraint at the `\one`-comparison-equality boundary of `conv:basics`. **No new GLOSSARY entries added** (per orchestrator instruction; both referenced terms already exist: `def:particle-number:507`, `conv:basics:130`; ONE of the two slugs has an explicit pre-bound P5.3 Configurations.lean canonical-CAD-anchor line at `GLOSSARY.md:536` (`def:particle-number`'s Translation map CAD section names this file verbatim + flags the reverse-decoupling caveat now discharged) — this commit completes the SINGLE GLOSSARY-pre-registered slug-to-file binding for `def:particle-number` AND discharges the GLOSSARY-tracked reverse-decoupling caveat). **Formalisation.lean update:** inserted one line `import Formalisation.Foundations.Configurations` immediately BEFORE the existing `import Formalisation.Foundations.DirectSumCoordinates` line (alphabetical within the Foundations block: `Configurations` < `DirectSumCoordinates` < `SkeletalFusion`), preserving the Phase-5 import-ordering convention established at P5.1 (Foundations BEFORE LinearAlgebra) AND the within-block flat alphabetical convention; `Formalisation.lean` grows 27 lines → 28 lines. **`lake build`** (post-port): "Built Formalisation.Foundations.Configurations (6.7s)" → "Built Formalisation (5.9s)" → "Build completed successfully (8451 jobs)"; exit 0; wall clock 22.537s real / 17.968s user / 8.831s sys. This file is the GLOSSARY-pre-registered canonical CAD support construction for `def:Hlatt` — verbatim per the Translation map CAD section at `GLOSSARY.md:497`: "Supporting CAD constructions on the same `H_N^W` skeleton: `Foundations/DirectSumCoordinates.lean` (Phase 5 P5.2) for the Σ↔Π sum equivalence; `Foundations/ConfigurationSpace.lean` (P5.4) for `summary.tex` §4.2 sector expansion". The `summary.tex` §4.2 sector expansion is realised here as the linear equivalence `configSpaceLinearEquiv : ConfigSpaceCoordinates basis ≃ₗ[ℂ] ConfigComponentCoordinates basis`: the flattened coordinate vector over all `(configuration, basis-vector-of-that-sector)` pairs is linearly equivalent to a per-configuration coordinate family. This packages the second-layer biproduct of the configuration-space decomposition `Hh_N^W = ⊕_{cfg} Hom_C(W, A_cfg)`. The underlying mechanism is `sigmaPiLinearEquiv` from P5.2's `DirectSumCoordinates.lean` (cited explicitly in `configSpaceLinearEquiv`'s body `:= sigmaPiLinearEquiv`), specialised here to the configuration index type `Config α n = Fin n → α` from P5.3's `Configurations.lean`. The dimension formula `configSpace_card_components` is the coordinate realisation of `dim Hh_N^W = ∑_cfg dim Hom_C(W, A_cfg)`, and its uniform-basis specialisation `configSpace_card_constant_basis` recovers the `|α|^n` site-count factor from P5.3's `card_configurations`. The isometry statement `configSpaceLinearEquiv_preserves_coordinatePairing` states that this expansion is an orthogonal direct sum at the coordinate-pairing level. (2) `def:particle-number` (GLOSSARY.md:507) — Particle number. This file does NOT itself define a particle-number function (P5.3 does), but it IS a consumer of `def:particle-number`'s underlying `Config α n` substrate: the `basis : Config α n → Type v` is indexed by exactly the same `Config α n = Fin n → α` from P5.3. The configuration-space sum is implicitly over the `def:particle-number`-stratified space `Config α n`. (3) `conv:basics` (GLOSSARY.md:130) — Notation and conventions. The complex-vector-space default is invoked throughout (every coordinate space is `→ ℂ`; `configSpaceLinearEquiv` is `≃ₗ[ℂ]`). The dagger / star pairing is inherited transparently through `configSpaceLinearEquiv_preserves_coordinatePairing`'s consumption of `sigmaCoordinatePairing` and `piCoordinatePairing` from P5.2. The `noncomputable section` opening (source line 18) is the standard Mathlib idiom inherited from the underlying `sigmaPiLinearEquiv` of P5.2. This file is the GLOSSARY-pre-registered canonical CAD support construction for `def:Hlatt` — verbatim per the Translation map CAD section at `GLOSSARY.md:497`: "Supporting CAD constructions on the same `H_N^W` skeleton: `Foundations/DirectSumCoordinates.lean` (Phase 5 P5.2) for the Σ↔Π sum equivalence; `Foundations/ConfigurationSpace.lean` (P5.4) for `summary.tex` §4.2 sector expansion; `Foundations/FockSpace.lean` (P5.5) for `summary.tex` §4.3 truncated-Fock-space view". The `summary.tex` §4.3 truncated-Fock-space view is realised here as the linear equivalence `truncatedFockLengthExpansion : TruncatedFockCoordinates localBasis maxN ≃ₗ[ℂ] TruncatedFockComponentCoordinates localBasis maxN`: the flattened coordinate vector over all `(particle-number, length-n word)` pairs is linearly equivalent to a per-particle-number coordinate family. The truncated-Fock basis is the sigma type `Σ (n : ParticleNumberUpTo maxN), Config localBasis n.val`, packaging the layered direct-sum expansion `F_{≤ maxN}(V_local) = ⊕_{n=0}^{maxN} V_local^{⊗n}` at coordinate level (each `V_local^{⊗n}` realised via P5.3's `Config localBasis n = Fin n → localBasis`). The dimension formula `truncatedFockBasis_card : Fintype.card (TruncatedFockBasis localBasis maxN) = ∑ n, Fintype.card localBasis ^ n.val` is the coordinate-level realisation of `dim F_{≤ maxN} = ∑ (dim V_local)^n`, the truncated geometric-sum dimension of the distinguishable-particle Fock space. Boundary specialisations `zeroParticleSector_card : Fintype.card (Config localBasis 0) = 1` (vacuum sector) and `oneParticleSector_card : Fintype.card (Config localBasis 1) = Fintype.card localBasis` (single-particle sector) record the `n=0` and `n=1` slices. The isometry statement `truncatedFockLengthExpansion_preserves_coordinatePairing` says the expansion is an isometry of coordinate pairings inherited from P5.2 — coordinate-level orthogonal direct sum. (2) `def:particle-number` (GLOSSARY.md:507) — Particle number. This file's `ParticleNumberUpTo maxN := Fin (maxN + 1)` is the canonical coordinate-skeleton index type for the truncated particle-number stratification of the distinguishable Fock space: it indexes the particle-number slices `n ∈ {0, 1, …, maxN}` over which `TruncatedFockBasis` is the sigma type `Σ n : ParticleNumberUpTo maxN, Config localBasis n.val`. This file does NOT itself define a particle-number FUNCTION (that is P5.3's `Foundations/Configurations.lean::Config.particleNumber`); rather, it uses the index type as the outer label of the truncated direct sum. (3) `def:mobile-Fock` (GLOSSARY.md:1940) — Mobile-Fock Hilbert space (MMA formulation). The OUTER ⊕_{N=0}^{L} layer of mobile-Fock (the particle-number / non-vacuum-leg-count direct sum, truncated at lattice length `L`) is the SAME direct-sum-structure-over-particle-number that this file formalises as `TruncatedFockBasis localBasis maxN`, with the MMA-side `L ↔ maxN` correspondence (the two are equivalent under vacuum-leg absorption per the [[def:mobile-Fock]] vs [[def:Hlatt]] translation map at GLOSSARY.md:1993-2001). This file's coordinate-skeleton realisation is on the `def:Hlatt` side of the equivalence (per the GLOSSARY.md:497 explicit pre-binding of this file to the `def:Hlatt` Translation map's CAD "Supporting CAD constructions on the same `H_N^W` skeleton" line as the P5.5 anchor for "`summary.tex` §4.3 truncated-Fock-space view"); `def:mobile-Fock` is the MMA-framing companion whose outer particle-number direct sum agrees with this file's outer sigma layer. No direct CAD formalisation of mobile-Fock itself is present (per GLOSSARY.md:2022: "CAD: not directly formalised"); this file is the truncated-Fock view of the `def:Hlatt` coordinate skeleton. (4) `conv:basics` (GLOSSARY.md:130) — Notation and conventions. Complex vector-space default (every coordinate space `→ ℂ`; `truncatedFockLengthExpansion` is `≃ₗ[ℂ]`). Dagger / star pairing inherited via `truncatedFockLengthExpansion_preserves_coordinatePairing`'s consumption of P5.2's `sigmaCoordinatePairing` / `piCoordinatePairing`. `noncomputable section` opening inherited from P5.2's `sigmaPiLinearEquiv`. `classical` tactic in `truncatedFockBasis_card`. ## Corrections

## Deviations from MIGRATION_PLAN.md

- **P0.6 subsumed by P0.1.** Plan had P0.6 as "add .gitignore + remove tracked build artifacts." Because P0.1 wrote `.gitignore` before `git add`, no build artifacts were ever tracked, so the `git rm --cached` step is unnecessary. P0.6 is marked subsumed.
- **P0.1b added.** `bd init` auto-creates files and auto-commits. Recorded as its own step.
- **P0.1c added.** Reconciliation of bd's auto-added CLAUDE/AGENTS sections with the user-approved Beads section.
- **P2.7 deviation: infrastructure pointer routed to PROVENANCE.md + README.md instead of CONVENTIONS.md per user adjudication 2026-05-16.** Rationale: CONVENTIONS.md docstring scope is notational/gauge/indexing modelling choices; infrastructure pointers do not fit. Plan text in MIGRATION_PLAN.md:157 should be updated correspondingly in a future doc-sync pass (file bd issue).
- **P3.0 added as prerequisite for P3.2 `\cite{SRC-*}` discharges.** Plan (`stocktake/MIGRATION_PLAN.md:170-176`) jumps from P3.1 (list emission) to P3.2 (per-flag discharge with `\cite{SRC-XYZ}`), implicitly assuming a `\begin{thebibliography}` infrastructure existed in `summary.tex`; in fact `summary.tex` had no `thebibliography` environment, no `\bibitem`, no `\cite{}` (verified by grep at commit `1113ddc` for the P2.8 CITATION_INDEX build; see CITATION_INDEX.md "Citation atom unit" section). User-adjudicated routing 2026-05-16: `\begin{thebibliography}` + `\cite` per plan literal (not a custom `\src{}` macro; not inline `\href{}`); per-atom granularity for P3.2 (3 commits for 3 dischargeable atoms). P3.0 added 5 `\bibitem` entries (SRC-GOLDEN-CHAIN, SRC-OAR-FERMIONS, SRC-OAR-WAVELETS, SRC-OSBORNE-CONTINUUM, SRC-STRING-NET) — purely additive insertion before `\end{document}`. Plan text in `MIGRATION_PLAN.md:170-176` should be updated correspondingly in a future doc-sync pass (parallel to P2.7's MIGRATION_PLAN doc-sync follow-up).
- **P3.4 plan-vs-reality observation: count-metric ambiguity in "decreased by exactly the count of P3.2 atomic steps".** Plan literal at `stocktake/MIGRATION_PLAN.md:174` says "verify the count of `\unchecked` flags decreased by exactly the count of P3.2 atomic steps." Under user-locked per-atom granularity for Phase 3, P3.2 ran as 3 atomic commits (`3403ca5` `osborne-stottmeister`, `c8d055b` `feiguin-golden-chain`, `c607efa` `string-net`) — so "P3.2 atomic steps" = 3. The actual measured `\unchecked`-macro-count delta is 26 → 21 = 5 instances (P3.2.a discharged 3 sites; P3.2.b discharged 1; P3.2.c discharged 1). Both numbers are coherent: the plan-literal check passes per per-atom interpretation (the per-step granularity was user-locked as per-atom, and 3 atomic commits actually shipped); the per-instance delta (5) is the stronger structural number. The discrepancy reflects the plan's writing-time implicit assumption that one `\unchecked` site per atom would be typical (true for 2 of the 3 dischargeable atoms — `feiguin-golden-chain` and `string-net` each had a single canonical-enumeration `\unchecked` — but not for `osborne-stottmeister`, which had 3 `\unchecked` sites: two inline-claim sites in §"Statements judged unverifiable" + Conjecture conj:KS, and the canonical-enumeration entry). No correction to plan needed; both readings record cleanly. Future plan-revision pass (parallel to P2.7 / P3.0 doc-sync follow-ups) may want to clarify the count metric as "per-atom granularity → 1 P3.2 atomic step per dischargeable atom; per-instance discharge count may exceed step count."
- **P4.1 plan-vs-reality observation: `lake update` on Lake 5.0.0 / Lean 4.30.0-rc2 modifies the canonical manifest.** Plan literal at `stocktake/MIGRATION_PLAN.md:184` says "Run `lake update` and `lake build` (empty)" and the orchestrator briefing said "Run `lake update`: resolves the dependency tree per `lake-manifest.json`. Should be fast (just reads manifest)." Empirically: the first `lake update` against the just-copied CAD manifest bumped the manifest schema version 1.1.0 → 1.2.0 (introducing the new top-level field `fixedToolchain: false`) and re-resolved Mathlib `d6dab93` → `e12bcd0` (drift along the `inputRev: null` default-branch tip) and batteries `5c57f38` → `48ff08a` (drift along `inputRev: "v4.30.0-rc2"` tag-tracking; the tag was retagged upstream after CAD's manifest was written). The drifted manifest was discarded by `cp`-restoring the canonical manifest from CAD (post-restore SHA256 `9622a638…` matches source byte-for-byte) and the per-package working trees in `.lake/packages/{mathlib,batteries}` were `git checkout`'d back to their canonical revisions; the other 7 transitive-dep working trees were already at their canonical pins (Lake's first-time resolve had matched their `inputRev` pins by chance). `lake exe cache get` was then re-run against the canonical Mathlib `d6dab93` and downloaded the matching 8418 cached oleans. **Lesson:** for P4.2–P4.14 (and subsequent Lean migrations), DO NOT run `lake update` — only `lake build` (and `lake exe cache get` if the cache needs repopulating). The manifest is the canonical pin; `lake update` should only be invoked with explicit user adjudication. The plan literal at `MIGRATION_PLAN.md:184` should be updated correspondingly in a future doc-sync pass (parallel to P2.7 / P3.0 / P3.4 doc-sync follow-ups; the cleanup batch grows).
- **P4.1 deviation: minimal `Formalisation.lean` placeholder created at repo root.** CAD's own `Formalisation.lean` (sibling repo SHA256 `5751ca84…`; 29 lines) is a full-tree re-export importing all `Foundations/`, `Fibonacci/`, `Ising/`, and `LinearAlgebra/` modules; copying it verbatim at P4.1 would fail to build because none of the imported modules exist yet (they land one-per-commit P4.2 through P4.14, with Phase-5 `Foundations/` / `Fibonacci/` / `Ising/` later). With the empty `Formalisation/` directory (only `.gitkeep`), `lake build` fails with "no such file or directory: Formalisation.lean" because the `lean_lib Formalisation` declaration in `lakefile.lean` requires a root file. A minimal 9-line comment-only placeholder was written (SHA256 `dafacfc7…`) to satisfy Lake's requirement; the comment documents the post-Phase-5 invariant ("`lake build` passes; zero `sorry`; zero `axiom`") and the per-P4.* `import` accumulation plan. Each P4.2–P4.14 commit will append one `import Formalisation.LinearAlgebra.<file>` line. CAD's tree-spanning re-export (or its `LinearAlgebra/`-only subset) becomes natural at P4.14 close; at that point the placeholder comment block can be trimmed in the same atomic commit that lands the last `LinearAlgebra/` file (or in a deliberate cleanup commit). No `lakefile.lean` adjustment needed — its `lean_lib Formalisation` line is preserved verbatim from CAD.
